# Faction leader convenes a meeting
character_event = {
	id = 1900500
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	desc = "EVTDESC1900500"	

	trigger = {
		had_global_flag = {
			flag = startup
			days = 730
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }	
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}	
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed }
			had_character_flag = {
				flag = faction_meeting_postponed
				days = 730
			}
			AND = {
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting_postponed
					days = 365
				}	
				NOT = {
					liege = {
						any_war = {
							defender = {
								character = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}	
				}				
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 						
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry					
						}
					}
				}					
			}				
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting }
			had_character_flag = {
				flag = faction_meeting
				days = 1095
			}
			AND = {
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting
					days = 730
				}	
				NOT = {
					liege = {
						any_war = {
							defender = {
								character = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}	
				}					
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry 						
						}
					}
				}		
			}			
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}	
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
					in_faction = faction_republican_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
					in_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}	
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
					in_faction = faction_religious_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
					in_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}	
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_court_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
					in_faction = faction_court_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
					in_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting
					days = 2555
				}
			}
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			NOT = {
				liege = {
					any_war = {
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}	
			}				
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 					
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 					
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 					
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry 					
					}
				}
			}
		}		
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900500"
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0 }
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke	
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP51 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke	
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP52 }
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke	
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP53 }
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke	
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP54 }
		}		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900502 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 1900503 days = 7 } # regular meeting
			character_event = { id = 1900504 days = 7 } # angry meeting		
		}		 
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1900500"
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10 
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0.5 }
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 }
			}				
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP50 }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				character_event = { id = 1900501 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}				
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				character_event = { id = 1900501 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}				
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				character_event = { id = 1900501 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}				
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 1900501 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }			
		}		
		change_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1 }		
	}	
}

character_event = {
	id = 1900501
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
	
	desc = "EVTDESC1900501"
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900518 } #notify
			}
		}	
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900501"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}			
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 1900502
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900502"	
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900502"
	}
}

# Regular meeting - setting the agenda
character_event = {
	id = 1900503
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900503"	
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }	
		has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						OR = { 
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 
						}						
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						OR = { 
							has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 
						}						
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						OR = { 
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 
						}						
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						OR = { 
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry 
						}						
					}
				}
			}
		}					
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}	
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
					in_faction = faction_republican_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
					in_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}	
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
					in_faction = faction_religious_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
					in_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}	
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_court_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
					in_faction = faction_court_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
					in_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
		}		
	}		
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge_defeated
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900503"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}				
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = humble
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = content
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = charitable
			}				
		}
		character_event = { id = 1900600 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900600 } #strengthen own position
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1900503"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = ambitious
			}				
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = proud
			}				
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = envious
			}				
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = { who = liege value = 100 }
			}							
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = { who = liege value = 75 }
			}							
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = { who = liege value = 50 }
			}					
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = { who = liege value = 25 }
			}							
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { opinion = { who = liege value = 0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { opinion = { who = liege value = -25 } }

				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900516 } }
				}
			}					
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } }
			}
			custom_tooltip = { 
				text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900516 } }	
			}
		}			
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge			
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTF1900504"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP59 }
		trigger = {
			liege = {
				any_war = {
					defender = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry				
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_court_angry				
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry					
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry				
					}
				}
			}			
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}	
}

# Faction leader is ousted after losing a regular vote
character_event = {
	id = 1900505
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900505"
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900519 } #notify
			}
		}	
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900505"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}			
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 1900506
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = "EVTDESC1900506"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900506"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_religious_king
				leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_republican_king
				leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_court_king
				leads_faction = faction_court_duke
			}			
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.49 } } }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.74 } } }
			}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5.0
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } }
			}				
			modifier = {
				factor = 100.0
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 2.99 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = craven
			}	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {

							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor

							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor

							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}

					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900904 } #vote
			}	
		}
		character_event = { id = 1900737 days = 7 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900737 }			
	}

# Faction leader is ousted after wasting a meeting
character_event = {
	id = 1900516
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900516"
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900520 } #notify
			}
		}		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900516"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}			
	}
}

		name = "EVTOPTA1900600"	# praise self in speech
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		trigger = {

		}		
		ai_chance = {

				trait = proud
			}

# Agenda - weaken liege
character_event = {
	id = 1900602
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900602"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900602"	# denounce liege in speech	
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				trait = humble
			}					
		}		
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		trigger = {
			diplomacy = 8
			NOT = { trait = stutter }
		}		
		random_list = {
			30 = { character_event = { id = 1900728 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900728 } } # faction opinion of liege decreased
			40 = { character_event = { id = 1900731 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900731 } } # faction opinion of liege slightly decreased
			30 = { character_event = { id = 1900734 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900734 } } # faction opinion of liege increased
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900602"	# denounce liege in speech

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				trait = proud
			}

				trait = humble
			}					
		}

				NOT = { diplomacy = 8 }
				trait = stutter
			 }
		}

			30 = { character_event = { id = 1900731 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900731 } } # faction opinion of liege slightly decreased
			50 = { character_event = { id = 1900734 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900734 } } # faction opinion of liege increased

# Great speech
character_event = {
	id = 1900700
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900700"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900700"
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = 200
		}		
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}						
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = great_speech	
				}	
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = good_speech	
				}	
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = okay_speech	
				}	
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = bad_speech	
				}		
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = terrible_speech	
				}						
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = great_speech
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900701 } } #notify
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}
}

# Awful speech
character_event = {
	id = 1900708
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900708"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900708"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}						
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = great_speech	
				}	
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = good_speech	
				}	
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = okay_speech	
				}	
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = bad_speech	
				}		
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = terrible_speech	
				}					
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = terrible_speech
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900709 } } #notify	
		}	
	}
}

# Faction leader wants money - result of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1900710
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900710"
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900710"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}	
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}						
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { tier = king } ROOT = { wealth = 30 } }
			if = { limit = { tier = duke } ROOT = { wealth = 20 } }
			if = { limit = { tier = count } ROOT = { wealth = 10 } }
		}	
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }	
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}				
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900711 } #notify
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1900710"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 } }
		}	
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }	
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900712 } #notify
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 33
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900505 days = 3 } }
		}		
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}	
}

character_event = {

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900713"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900713"

			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900714 } #notify
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = 3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900715 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = 3 }	
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900715 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_republican" value = 3 }	
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900715 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = 3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900715 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}		
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}
}

	id = 1900716
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900716"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900716"		
		hidden_tooltip = { 	
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900717 } #notify
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = 1 }	
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900718 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = 1 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }		
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900718 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_republican" value = 1 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900718 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = 1 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }	
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900718 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}		
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}
}

# Decreased faction opinion of liege

	id = 1900719
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900719"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900719"		
		hidden_tooltip = { 	
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900720 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry				
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry				
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry				
						}
					}
				}	
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900505 days = 3 } }			
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy		
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy			
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy				
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy				
						}
					}
				}	
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900505 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
							}				
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
							}					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
							}					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy
							}	
						}
					}
				}	
			}
			random = {
				chance = 20
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900505 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = -3 }	
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900721 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = -3 }	
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900721 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_republican" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }				
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900721 } } #notify
				}
			}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = -3 }	
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900721 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}		
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}

# Faction leader wants money for liege - result of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1900722
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900722"
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900722"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		if = { limit = { tier = king } wealth = -30 }
		if = { limit = { tier = duke } wealth = -20 }
		if = { limit = { tier = count } wealth = -10 }			
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }	
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }	
		}				
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke

# Yes vote - notify
character_event = {
	id = 1900723
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900723"
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		if = { limit = { tier = king } wealth = -30 }
		if = { limit = { tier = duke } wealth = -20 }
		if = { limit = { tier = count } wealth = -10 }		
		FROM = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }	
			}
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }	
			}	
		}		
	}
}

							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy				
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy				
						}
					}
				}	
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900505 days = 3 } }				
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
							}				
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
							}					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
							}					
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy
							}	
						}
					}
				}	
			}
			random = {
				chance = 20
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900505 days = 3 } }				
			}
		}			
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}	
}

# Yes vote - notify
character_event = {
	id = 1900726
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900726"
	
	trigger = {	
		ai = no
	}		
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		FROM = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }		
			}
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
			}	
		}		
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 1900728
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900728"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900728"	
		hidden_tooltip = { 	
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900729 } #notify
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900730 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = -3 }	
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900730 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_republican" value = -3 }	
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900730 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = { 
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 110073 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900730 } } #notify
				}
			}	
		}		
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}

# Faction leader wants to declare war - results of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1900737
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900737"
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900737"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }		
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900738 } #notify
			}		
		}
		liege = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {	
					set_character_flag = faction_feudal_war
					ROOT = {
						add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { opinion = { who = LIEGE modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } }	
						any_faction_backer = {
							faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { opinion = { who = LIEGE modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } }					
						}
					}	
				}					
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = cb_faction_overthrow_ruler
					faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_character_flag = faction_feudal_war
					ROOT = {
						add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { opinion = { who = LIEGE modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } }

					limit = {

							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke					
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = 2000020 }
				}

				}

						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}	
					character_event = { id = 2000040 } 
				}	
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting

		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1900737"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 } }
		}	
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }	
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {

					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {

character_event = {

	hide_from = yes

	desc = "EVTDESC1900740"
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900740"

		}
		if = {

					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke

						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900745 } #notify
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900505 days = 3 } }
		}		
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}
