# Faction leader wants to demand a change in tax privilege - results of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1900746
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900746"
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900746"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke		
				}	
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1901051 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke		
				}	
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1902051 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke		
				}	
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1903051 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
				}	
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1904051 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}			
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }		
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900747 } #notify
			}		
		}			
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1900746"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 } }
		}	
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }	
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }	
		}		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900748 } #notify
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50
			custom_tooltip = { 
				text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1900505 days = 3 } }
			}
		}		
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed

	}

# Faction leader wants to demand a change in council law - results of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1900752
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"	
		
	desc = "EVTDESC1900752"
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900752"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke		
				}	
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1904041 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}			
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }

							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor

						AND = {

							in_faction = faction_republican_king

						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke

							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor

							in_faction = faction_religious_king

						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}

							in_faction = faction_court_duke

					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900753 } #notify
			}

		set_character_flag = faction_meeting

		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge		
	}
	option = {

		}

		any_playable_ruler = {

				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }

		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }

		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge_defeated }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke

			leads_faction = faction_religious_king

						value = 0
					}

							in_faction = faction_republican_king

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900803 } #notify
			}
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1900801"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 } }
		}	
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
		set_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge_defeated
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP48 }	
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }		
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP49 }
		}	
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}	
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}						
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1900804 } #notify
			}
		}		
	}
